	cin>>n;
	if(n>30)
		cout<<"out of range!";
	else{
	
		cout<<"enter the elements of array\n";
		for(i=1;i<=n;i++){
			cin>>ar[i];
		}
		for(i=1;i<=n;i++){
			cout<<"ar["<<i<<"]="<<ar[i]<<endl;
		}
		cout<<"enter the number you want to insert:";
		cin>>num;
		cout<<"enter the position: ";
		cin>>pos;
		for (i = n; i >= pos;i--){
		  	ar[i+1] = ar[i];
		    }
		ar[pos] = num;
		n++;
		for(i=1;i<=n;i++){
			cout<<"ar["<<i<<"]="<<ar[i]<<endl;
		}
		}
}

26/08/22, 10:25 pm - +91 6387 438 544: #include <cmath>
#include <cstdio>
#include <vector>
#include <iostream>
#include <algorithm>
using namespace std;


int main() {
    int i,a, max,index;
    cin>>a;
    int arr[a];
    for(i=0;i<a;i++){
        cin>>arr[i];
    }
    max = arr[0];
    for(i=1; i<a; i++){
        if(max < arr[i])
        max = arr[i];
    }
    for(i=a-1; i>=0; i--){
        if(arr[i]==max)
        {
            index = i;
            break;
        }
    }
    cout<<index;
    cout<<endl;

    return 0;
}

#include <cstdio>
#include <vector>
#include <iostream>
#include <algorithm>
using namespace std;
    /* Enter your code here. Read input from STDIN. Print output to STDOUT */ 
    void insertElement(char Arr[], int &n, char z, int m) 
    {
    for (int i = n; i > m; --i)
    {
        Arr[i] = Arr[i-1];
    }
    Arr[m] = z;
    ++n;
    }

int main () {
    int n; 
    int s ;
    cin >> s;
    if (s <= 0 || s > 20)
    {
        cout << "Invalid size of array" << endl;
        return 0;
    }
    char Arr[2*s];
    int i = 0;
    do
    {
        cin >> Arr[i];
        ++i;
    }while(Arr[i-1] != '\0');
    n = i-1;
    for (int i = 0; i < n; ++i)
    {
        if (Arr[i] >= 'A' && Arr[i] <= 'Z') 
        {
            insertElement(Arr, n, Arr[i]+32, i+1);
        }
    }
    for (int i = 0; i < n; ++i)
    {
        cout << Arr[i] << " ";
    }
    return 0;
}

using namespace std;
struct node
{
public:
int data;
node *next;
};
struct node *head=NULL;
void insert(int new_data)
{
struct node *new_node=new node;
new_node->data=new_data;
new_node->next=head;
head=new_node;
}
void display()
{
struct node *ptr;
ptr=head;
while(ptr!=NULL)
{
cout<<2*ptr->data<<endl;
ptr=ptr->next;
}
}
int main()
{
insert(4);
insert(3); insert(2);
insert(4);
insert(1);
cout<<"The linked list is: ";
display();
return 0;
}

Subject :   DAY SCHOLAR STUDENTS EXIT TIMINGS 

1.All Day Scholar Girls and Boys Students,  are hereby informed that,  they should exit from the Campus every day in the evenings by 6 PM.

2. Any Day Scholar Girl or Boy student  found within Campus after 6 PM  in the evenings,  he / she must have permission of DUTY LEAVE Leave from their Head of Division ( HD )  or  from their Head of School ( HOS )  in their mobiles,  which should be displayed to Security Staff at Main Gate before exit.   All students without  DUTY LEAVE will be dealt as indiscipline case.


3.   We request complete cooperation on these guide lines  from all of our students.


Authorized by
Division of Security & Safety

using namespace std;
struct node
{
public:
    int data;
    node *next;
};
struct node *head = NULL;
void insert(int new_data)
{
    struct node *new_node = new node;
    new_node->data = new_data;
    new_node->next = head;
    head = new_node;
}

int main()
{
    int temp = 0;
    int data;
    do
    {
        cin >> data;
        if (data != -1)
        {
            insert(data);
        }
    } while (data != -1);

    int count = 0;
    struct node *ptr;
    ptr = head;
    while (ptr != NULL)
    {
        if ((ptr->data) % 2 == 0)
        {
            count++;
            temp = 1;
        }
        ptr = ptr->next;
    }
    if (temp != 0)
    {
        cout << count;
    }
    else
    {
        cout << "No even number present";
    }
}

06/09/22, 7:34 pm - +91 72249 72033: #include <iostream>
using namespace std;
struct node
{
public:
    int data;
    node *next;
};
struct node *head = NULL;
void insert(int new_data)
{
    struct node *new_node = new node;
    new_node->data = new_data;
    new_node->next = head;
    head = new_node;
}

int main()
{
  
    int n;
    cin>>n;
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++)
    {
        int age;
        cin>>age;
        insert(age);
    }
    node *ptr;
    ptr=head;
    int count = 0,temp=0;
    while (ptr != NULL)
    {
        if ((ptr->data) > 18)
        {
            count++;
            temp = 1;
        }
        ptr = ptr->next;
    }
    if (temp != 0)
    {
        cout << count;
    }
    else
    {
        cout <<0;
    }
    
}

09/09/22, 9:45 am - +91 788 050 6337: #include <cmath>
#include <cstdio>
#include <vector>
#include <iostream>
#include <algorithm>
#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
struct node{
public:
int data;
node *ptr;
};
struct node *head = NULL;
void insert(int new_data)
{
struct node *new_node = new node;
new_node->data = new_data;
new_node->ptr = head;
head = new_node;
}
bool isPalin(){
struct node * slow= head;
stack <int> s;
while(slow != NULL){
int n = slow->data;
int reversed_number=0;
while(n != 0) {
int remainder = n % 10;
reversed_number = reversed_number * 10 + remainder;
n /= 10;
}
s.push(reversed_number);
slow = slow->ptr;
}
while(head != NULL ){
int i=s.top();
s.pop();
if(head -> data != i){
return false;
}
head=head->ptr;
}
return true;
}
int main(){
int n;
cin>>n;
if(n<5 or n>=15){
cout<<"Invalid Input";
return 0;
}
for (int i = 0; i < n; i++){
int num;
cin>>num;
insert(num);
}
int result = isPalin();
if(result == 1)
cout<<"Yes";
else
cout<<"No";
return 0;
}

13/09/22, 11:26 am - Nilesh Tech-a-thon: #include <cmath>
#include <cstdio>
#include <vector>
#include <iostream>
#include <algorithm>
using namespace std;

bool isPerfectSquare(int x)
{
    int s = sqrt(x);
    return (s * s == x);
}

bool isFibonacci(int n){
    return isPerfectSquare(5 * n * n + 4) || isPerfectSquare(5 * n * n - 4);
}

int main() {
    int n;
    cin>>n;
    int arr[n];
    vector<int> idx;
    for(int i=0; i<n; i++){
        cin>>arr[i];
        if(isFibonacci(arr[i])){
            idx.push_back(i);
        }
    }
    for(int i=0; i<n-1; i++){
        arr[idx[idx.size()-1]] = -1;
        idx.pop_back();
        for(int j=0; j<n; j++){
            if(arr[j]==-1)  continue;
            cout<<arr[j]<<" ";
        }
        cout<<endl;
    }
    return 0;
}
